create_access_token(data: Dict[str, Any], expires_delta: Optional[timedelta] = None) -> str:\n    """\n    Create a JWT access token\n    \n    Args:\n        data: Data to encode in the token\n        expires_delta: Optional expiration time delta\n        \n    Returns:\n        Encoded JWT token\n    """\n    to_encode = data.copy()\n    if expires_delta:\n        expire = datetime.utcnow() + expires_delta\n    else:\n        expire = datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(minutes=ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES)\n    \n    to_encode.update({"exp": expire})\n    encoded_jwt = jwt.encode(to_encode, JWT token to decode\n        \n    Returns:\n        Decoded token data\n        \n    Raises:\n        HTTPException: If token is invalid or expired\n    """\n    try:\n        payload = jwt.decode(token, SECRET_KEY, algorithms=[ALGORITHM])\n        return payload\n    except JWTError:\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,\n            detail="Could not validate credentials",\n            headers={"WWW-Authenticate": "Bearer"},\n        )\n\n\nasync def get_current_user(token: str = Depends(oauth2_scheme)) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    """\n    Get current user from JWT token\n    \n    Args:\n        token: JWT token from request\n        \n    Returns:\n        User data from token\n        \n    Raises:\n        HTTPException: If background_tasks: BackgroundTasks,\n    db: Session = Depends(get_db)\n):\n    """Create and start a new QA scan"""\n    \n    # Determine which products to scan\n    if request.product_ids:\n        products = db.query(Product).filter(\n            Product.id.in_(request.product_ids),\n            Product.is_active == True\n        ).all()\n    else:\n        products = db.query(Product).filter(Product.is_active == True).all()\n    \n    if not products:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="No active products found to scan")\n    \n    # Create scan record\n    scan = QAScan(\n        scan_type=request.scan_type,\n        triggered_by="api",\n        product_ids=[p.id for p in products],\n        check_categories=request.check_categories,\n        total_products=len(products),\n        started_at=datetime.utcnow(),\n        status="running",\n        config={\n            "auto_fix": request.auto_fix,\n            "environment": request.environment\n        }\n    )\n    \n    db.add(scan)\n    db.commit()\n    db.refresh(scan)\n    \n    # Run scan in background\n    background_tasks.add_task(\n        run_scan_task,\n        scan.id,\n        [p.name for p in products],\n        request.check_categories,\n        request.auto_fix\n    )\n    \n    return scan\n\n\nasync def run_scan_task(\n    scan_id: int,\n    product_names: List[str],\n    check_categories: Optional[List[str]],\n    auto_fix: bool\n):\n    """Background task to run the scan"""\n    from app.core.database import get_db_context\n    \n    with get_db_context() as db:\n        scan = db.query(QAScan).filter(QAScan.id == scan_id).first()\n        if not scan:\n            return\n        \n        try:\n            qa_engine = QAEngine()\n            \n            total_checks = 0\n            passed_checks = 0\n            failed_checks = 0\n            warning_checks = 0\n            skipped_checks = 0\n            auto_fixes_attempted = 0\n            auto_fixes_successful = 0\n            product_scores = []\n            \n            # Run checks for each product\n            for product_name in product_names:\n                results = await qa_engine.run_all_checks(product_name)\n                \n                for result in results:\n                    total_checks += 1\n                    \n                    if result["status"] == "passed":\n                        passed_checks += 1\n                    elif result["status"] == "failed":\n                        failed_checks += 1\n                        \n                        # Attempt auto-fix if enabled\n                        if auto_fix and result.get("can_auto_fix"):\n                            auto_fixes_attempted += 1\n                            fix_result = await qa_engine.auto_fix_issue(\n                                product_name,\n                                result["check_id"],\n                                result\n                            )\n                            if fix_result.get("success"):\n                                auto_fixes_successful += 1\n                    elif result["status"] == "warning":\n                        warning_checks += 1\n                    elif result["status"] == "skipped":\n                        skipped_checks += 1\n                \n                # Calculate product score\n                product = db.query(Product).filter(Product.name == product_name).first()\n                if product:\n                    product_scores.append(product.qa_score)\n            \n            # Calculate overall scores\n            overall_score = (passed_checks / total_checks * 100) if total_checks > 0 else 0\n            average_product_score = sum(product_scores) / len(product_scores) if product_scores else 0\n            \n            # Update scan record\n            scan.total_checks = total_checks\n            scan.passed_checks = passed_checks\n            scan.failed_checks = failed_checks\n            scan.warning_checks = warning_checks\n            scan.skipped_checks = skipped_checks\n            scan.overall_score = overall_score\n            scan.average_product_score = average_product_score\n            scan.auto_fixes_attempted = auto_fixes_attempted\n            scan.auto_fixes_successful = auto_fixes_successful\n            scan.completed_at = datetime.utcnow()\n            scan.duration_seconds = (scan.completed_at - scan.started_at).total_seconds()\n            scan.status = "completed"\n            scan.summary = {\n                "total_products": len(product_names),\n                "total_checks": total_checks,\n                "passed_checks": passed_checks,\n                "failed_checks": failed_checks,\n                "warning_checks": warning_checks,\n                "pass_rate": (passed_checks / total_checks * 100) if total_checks > 0 else 0,\n                "auto_fix_success_rate": (auto_fixes_successful / auto_fixes_attempted * 100) if auto_fixes_attempted > 0 else 0\n            }\n            \n            db.commit()\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            scan.status = "failed"\n            scan.completed_at = datetime.utcnow()\n            scan.duration_seconds = (scan.completed_at - scan.started_at).total_seconds()\n            scan.summary = {"error": str(e)}\n            db.commit()\n\n\n@router.get("/", completed_scans,\n        "running_scans": running_scans,\n        "failed_scans": failed_scans,\n        "average_overall_score": round(avg_overall_score, 2),\n        "average_product_score": round(avg_product_score, 2),\n        "latest_scan": {\n            "id": latest_scan.id,\n            "status": latest_scan.status,\n            "overall_score": latest_scan.overall_score,\n "system"\n\n\nclass TaskStatus(str, enum.Enum):\n    """Status of a task"""\n    TODO = "todo"\n    IN_PROGRESS = "in_progress"\n    REVIEW = "review"\n    DONE = "done"\n    BLOCKED = "blocked"\n\n\nclass AIRequestType(str, enum.Enum):\n    """Type of AI request"""\n    CODE_GENERATION = "code_generation"\n    APP_SCAFFOLDING = "app_scaffolding"\n    BUG_FIX = "bug_fix"\n    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, index=True)\n    email = Column(String(255), unique=True, nullable=False, index=True)\n    username = Column(String(100), unique=True, nullable=False, Column(Integer, primary_key=True, index=True)\n    name = Column(String(200), nullable=False, index=True)\n    description = Column(Text)\n    \n    # Status\n    status = ForeignKey("users.id"), nullable=False)\n    \n    # Metadata\n    tags = Column(JSON)\n    metadata = Column(JSON)\n    \n    # Timestamps\n    created_at = Column(DateTime, messages = relationship("Message", back_populates="project")\n    ai_requests = relationship("AIRequest", back_populates="project")\n    progress_updates = relationship("ProgressUpdate",    \n    # Role in project\n    role = Column(String(100))  # Developer, Designer, PM, etc.\n    permissions = Column(JSON)  # List of permissions\n    \n    # Status\n    is_active = Column(Boolean, default=True)\n    joined_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)\n    left_at = Column(DateTime)\n    \n    # Relationships\n    project = relationship("Project", # List of file URLs\n    \n    # Thread\n    parent_message_id = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("messages.id"))\n    thread_count = Column(Integer, default=0)\n    \n    # Reactions\n    reactions = Column(JSON)  # List of user IDs mentioned\n    \n    # Timestamps\n    created_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)\n    updated_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow, Task(Base):\n    """Task model"""\n    __tablename__ = "tasks"\n\n    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, index=True)\n    project_id = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("projects.id"), nullable=False)\n    \n    # Task details\n    title = Column(String(200), nullable=False)\n    description = Column(Text)\n    status = Column(SQLEnum(TaskStatus), default=TaskStatus.TODO)\n    priority = Column(SQLEnum(ProjectPriority), default=ProjectPriority.MEDIUM)\n    \n    # Assignment\n    assignee_id = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("users.id"))\n    \n    # Estimates\n    estimated_hours = Column(Float)\n    actual_hours = Column(Float, default=0.0)\n    \n    # Dates\n    due_date = Column(DateTime)\n    completed_date = Column(DateTime)\n    \n    # Dependencies\n    depends_on = Column(JSON)  # List of task IDs\n    blocks = Column(JSON)  # List of task IDs\n    \n    # Metadata\n    tags = Column(JSON)\n    checklist = Column(JSON)  # List of subtasks\n    \n    # Timestamps\n    created_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)\n    updated_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow, onupdate=datetime.utcnow)\n    \n    # Relationships\n    project = relationship("Project", back_populates="tasks")\n    assignee = relationship("User", back_populates="tasks_assigned", foreign_keys=[assignee_id])\n\n\nclass AIRequest(Base):\n    """AI request model for SuperNinja Agent"""\n    __tablename__ = "ai_requests"\n\n    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, index=True)\n    project_id = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("projects.id"), nullable=False)\n nullable=False)\n    context = Column(JSON)  # Additional context\n    \n    # Response\n    response = Column(Text)\n    generated_code = Column(Text)\n    generated_files = Column(JSON)  # List of generated files\n    \n    # Status\n    status = Column(String(50), default="pending")  # pending, processing, completed, failed\n    progress = Column(Float, default=0.0)\n    \n    # Execution\n    execution_time_seconds = Column(Float)\n    tokens_used = Column(Integer)\n    \n    # Result\n    success = Column(Boolean)\n    error_message = Column(Text)\n    \n    # Metadata\n    metadata = Column(JSON)\n    \n    # Timestamps\n    created_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)\n    completed_at = Column(DateTime)\n    \n    # Relationships\n    project = relationship("Project",
